<pr_description>
Using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from defineConsts
### Describe the issue

When using a dynamic function as a style value in `stylex.create` together with a constants from a StyleX constants file (`defineConsts`), the following error occurs:

```bash
/stylex/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js: Invalid pseudo or at-rule.

      68 |       )
      69 |     ) {
    > 70 |       throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
         |             ^
      71 |     }
      72 |     if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      73 |       throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:70:13)
      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:42:9)
      at styleXCreateSet (src/shared/stylex-create.js:57:22)
      at transformStyleXCreate (src/visitors/stylex-create.js:169:19)
      at PluginPass.CallExpression (src/index.js:311:30)
      at call (../../../node_modules/@babel/traverse/src/visitors.ts:303:14)

```

### Expected behavior

Correct style transformation using constants as dynamic styles

### Steps to reproduce

Add styles as in `test case` section

### Test case

```js
// packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/transform-stylex-defineConsts-test.js

test('dynamic styles with StyleX constants', () => {
      const { code, } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
        import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
        import { mediaQueries } from './constants.stylex';

        export const styles = stylex.create({
          nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
            transition: {
              [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
              default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
            },
          }),
        });
      `);

      expect(code).toMatchInlineSnapshot(`
        "
          // Transformation result
        "
      `);
    });
```

### Additional comments

Thanks to @martinbooth for discovering and [reporting](https://github.com/Dwlad90/stylex-swc-plugin/issues/504) this bug

   189	      const dynamicFnsNames = Object.values(fns)
   190	        ?.map((entry) =>
   191	          Object.entries(entry[1]).map(([variableName, obj]) => ({
   192	            variableName,
   193	            path: obj.path,
   194	          })),
   195	        )
   196	        .flat();
   197	
   198	      dynamicFnsNames.forEach(({ variableName, path }) => {
   199	        // Pseudo elements can only access css vars via inheritance
   200	        const isPseudoElement = path.some((p) => p.startsWith('::'));
   201	        injectedInheritStyles[variableName] = {
   202	          priority: 0,
   203	          ltr: `@property ${variableName} { syntax: "*";${isPseudoElement ? '' : ' inherits: false;'}}`,
   204	          rtl: null,
   205	        };
   206	      });
   207	    }

   210	    let [compiledStyles, injectedStylesSansKeyframes, classPathsPerNamespace] =

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.

    10	/**
    11	 * This is a extended version of the path evaluation code from Babel.
    12	 *
    13	 * The original can be found at:
    14	 * https://github.com/babel/babel/blob/main/packages/babel-traverse/src/path/evaluation.ts
    15	 *
    16	 * The following extensions were made:
    17	 * - It can accept a mapping from variable names to functions
    18	 *   which when encountered will be evaluated instead of deopting.
    19	 *   - The functions can be configured to accept the raw path instead of
    20	 *     static values to handle dynamic values.
    21	 * - It can handle object spreads when the spread value itself is statically evaluated.
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import type { NodePath, Binding } from '@babel/traverse';
    25	
    26	import { parseSync } from '@babel/core';
    27	import traverse from '@babel/traverse';
    28	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    29	import StateManager from './state-manager';
    30	import { utils } from '../shared';
    31	import * as errMsgs from './evaluation-errors';
    32	
    33	// This file contains Babels metainterpreter that can evaluate static code.
    34	
    35	const VALID_CALLEES = ['String', 'Number', 'Math', 'Object', 'Array'];
    36	const INVALID_METHODS = [
    37	  'random',
    38	  'assign',
    39	  'defineProperties',
    40	  'defineProperty',
    41	  'freeze',
    42	  'seal',
    43	  'splice',
    44	];
    45	
    46	function isValidCallee(val: string): boolean {
    47	  return (VALID_CALLEES as $ReadOnlyArray<string>).includes(val);
    48	}
    49	
    50	function isInvalidMethod(val: string): boolean {
    51	  return INVALID_METHODS.includes(val);
    52	}
    53	
    54	export type FunctionConfig = {
    55	  identifiers: {
    56	    [fnName: string]: $FlowFixMe,
    57	  },
    58	  memberExpressions: {
    59	    [key: string]: {
    60	      [memberName: string]: {
    61	        fn: (...args: $FlowFixMe[]) => $FlowFixMe,
    62	        takesPath?: boolean,
    63	      },
    64	    },
    65	  },
    66	};
    67	
    68	type State = {
    69	  confident: boolean,
    70	  deoptPath: NodePath<> | null,
    71	  deoptReason?: string,
    72	  seen: Map<t.Node, Result>,
    73	  addedImports: Set<string>,
    74	  functions: FunctionConfig,
    75	  traversalState: StateManager,
    76	};
    77	
    78	type Result =
    79	  | {
    80	      resolved: true,
    81	      value: any,
    82	    }
    83	  | {
    84	      resolved: false,
    85	      reason: string,
    86	    };
    87	/**
    88	 * Deopts the evaluation
    89	 */
    90	function deopt(path: NodePath<>, state: State, reason: string): void {
    91	  if (!state.confident) return;
    92	  state.deoptPath = path;
    93	  state.confident = false;
    94	  state.deoptReason = reason;
    95	}
    96	
    97	function evaluateImportedFile(
    98	  filePath: string,
    99	  namedExport: string,
   100	  state: State,
   101	  bindingPath: NodePath<>,
   102	): any {
   103	  const fs = require('fs');
   104	  const fileContents = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   105	  // It's safe to use `.babelrc` here because we're only
   106	  // interested in the JS runtime, and not the CSS.
   107	  // TODO: in environments where `.babelrc` is not available,
   108	  // we need to find a way to decide whether to use Flow or TS syntax extensions.
   109	  const ast: null | t.File | { +errors: mixed } = parseSync(fileContents, {
   110	    babelrc: true,
   111	  });
   112	  if (!ast || ast.errors || !t.isNode(ast)) {
   113	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_PARSING_ERROR);
   114	    return;
   115	  }
   116	
   117	  const astNode: t.Node = ast as $FlowFixMe;
   118	
   119	  let result: any;
   120	
   121	  traverse(astNode, {
   122	    ExportNamedDeclaration(path: NodePath<t.ExportNamedDeclaration>) {
   123	      const declaration = path.get('declaration');
   124	
   125	      if (declaration.isVariableDeclaration()) {
   126	        const decls = declaration.get('declarations');
   127	
   128	        const finder = (decl: NodePath<t.Node>) => {
   129	          if (decl.isVariableDeclarator()) {
   130	            const id = decl.get('id');
   131	            const init: ?NodePath<t.Expression> = (
   132	              decl as NodePath<t.VariableDeclarator>
   133	            ).get('init');
   134	            if (
   135	              id.isIdentifier() &&
   136	              id.node.name === namedExport &&
   137	              init != null &&
   138	              init.isExpression()
   139	            ) {
   140	              result = evaluateCached(init, state);
   141	            }
   142	          }
   143	        };
   144	        if (Array.isArray(decls)) {
   145	          decls.forEach(finder);
   146	        } else {
   147	          finder(decls);
   148	        }
   149	      }
   150	    },
   151	  });
   152	
   153	  if (state.confident) {
   154	    return result;
   155	  } else {
   156	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   157	    return;
   158	  }
   159	}
   160	
   161	function evaluateThemeRef(
   162	  fileName: string,
   163	  exportName: string,
   164	  state: State,
   165	): { [key: string]: string } {
   166	  const resolveKey = (key: string) => {
   167	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
   168	      return `var(${key})`;
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    const strToHash =
   172	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   173	        ? utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName })
   174	        : utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName, key });
   175	
   176	    const { debug, enableDebugClassNames } = state.traversalState.options;
   177	
   178	    const varSafeKey =
   179	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   180	        ? ''
   181	        : (key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key).replace(
   182	            /[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,
   183	            '_',
   184	          ) + '-';
   185	
   186	    const varName =
   187	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
   188	        ? varSafeKey +
   189	          state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix +
   190	          utils.hash(strToHash)
   191	        : state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix + utils.hash(strToHash);
   192	
   193	    if (key === '__varGroupHash__') {
   194	      return varName;
   195	    }
   196	    return `var(--${varName})`;
   197	  };
   198	
   199	  // A JS proxy that uses the key to generate a string value using the `resolveKey` function
   200	  const proxy = new Proxy(
   201	    {},
   202	    {
   203	      get(_, key: string) {
   204	        return resolveKey(key);
   205	      },
   206	      set(_, key: string, value: string) {
   207	        throw new Error(
   208	          `Cannot set value ${value} to key ${key} in theme ${fileName}`,
   209	        );
   210	      },
   211	    },
   212	  );
   213	
   214	  return proxy;
   215	}
   216	
   217	/**
   218	 * We wrap the _evaluate method so we can track `seen` nodes, we push an item
   219	 * to the map before we actually evaluate it so we can deopt on self recursive
   220	 * nodes such as:
   221	 *
   222	 *   var g = a ? 1 : 2,
   223	 *       a = g * this.foo
   224	 */
   225	function evaluateCached(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   226	  const { node } = path;
   227	  const { seen } = state;
   228	
   229	  const existing: ?Result = seen.get(node);
   230	  if (existing != null) {
   231	    if (existing.resolved) {
   232	      return existing.value;
   233	    } else {
   234	      deopt(path, state, existing.reason);
   235	      return;
   236	    }
   237	  } else {
   238	    const item: Result = { resolved: false, reason: 'Currently evaluating' };
   239	    seen.set(node, item);
   240	
   241	    if (node == null) {
   242	      deopt(path, state, errMsgs.PATH_WITHOUT_NODE);
   243	      return;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    const val = _evaluate(path, state);
   247	    if (state.confident) {
   248	      seen.set(node, {
   249	        resolved: true,
   250	        value: val,
   251	      });
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    return val;
   255	  }
   256	}
   257	
   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260	
   261	  if (path.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
   262	    const body = path.get('body');
   263	    const params: $ReadOnlyArray<
   264	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   265	    > = path.get('params');
   266	    const identParams = params
   267	      .filter(
   268	        (
   269	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   270	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
   271	      )
   272	      .map((paramPath) => paramPath.node.name);
   273	    if (body.isExpression() && identParams.length === params.length) {
   274	      const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = body;
   275	      return (...args) => {
   276	        const identifierEntries = identParams.map(
   277	          (ident, index): [string, any] => [ident, args[index]],
   278	        );
   279	        const identifiersObj = Object.fromEntries(identifierEntries);
   280	        const result = evaluate(expr, state.traversalState, {
   281	          ...state.functions,
   282	          identifiers: { ...state.functions.identifiers, ...identifiersObj },
   283	        });
   284	        return result.value;
   285	      };
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  if (path.isIdentifier()) {
   290	    const name: string = path.node.name;
   291	    if (Object.keys(state.functions?.identifiers ?? {}).includes(name)) {
   292	      return state.functions.identifiers[name];
   293	    }
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  if (path.isTSAsExpression()) {
   297	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = path.get('expression');
   298	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  if (path.node.type === 'TSSatisfiesExpression') {
   302	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = (path as $FlowFixMe).get('expression');
   303	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   304	  }
   305	
   306	  if (path.isSequenceExpression()) {
   307	    const exprs = path.get('expressions');
   308	    return evaluateCached(exprs[exprs.length - 1], state);
   309	  }
   310	
   311	  if (
   312	    path.isStringLiteral() ||
   313	    path.isNumericLiteral() ||
   314	    path.isBooleanLiteral()
   315	  ) {
   316	    return path.node.value;
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  if (path.isNullLiteral()) {
   320	    return null;
   321	  }
   322	
   323	  if (path.isTemplateLiteral()) {
   324	    return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasis, state);
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  const maybeTag = path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() && path.get('tag');
   328	  if (
   329	    path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() &&
   330	    maybeTag &&
   331	    maybeTag.isMemberExpression()
   332	  ) {
   333	    const tag: NodePath<t.MemberExpression> = maybeTag;
   334	    const object: NodePath<t.Expression | t.Super> = tag.get('object');
   335	
   336	    if (object.isIdentifier()) {
   337	      const name = object.node.name;
   338	      const property: NodePath<> = tag.get('property');
   339	
   340	      if (
   341	        name === 'String' &&
   342	        !path.scope.hasBinding(name) &&
   343	        property.isIdentifier() &&
   344	        property.node.name === 'raw'
   345	      ) {
   346	        return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasi.quasis, state, true);
   347	      }
   348	    }
   349	  }
   350	
   351	  if (path.isConditionalExpression()) {
   352	    const testResult = evaluateCached(path.get('test'), state);
   353	    if (!state.confident) return;
   354	    if (testResult) {
   355	      return evaluateCached(path.get('consequent'), state);

   882	/**
   883	 * Walk the input `node` and statically evaluate it.
   884	 *
   885	 * Returns an object in the form `{ confident, value, deopt }`. `confident`
   886	 * indicates whether or not we had to drop out of evaluating the expression
   887	 * because of hitting an unknown node that we couldn't confidently find the
   888	 * value of, in which case `deopt` is the path of said node.
   889	 *
   890	 * Example:
   891	 *
   892	 *   evaluate(parse("5 + 5")) // { confident: true, value: 10 }
   893	 *   evaluate(parse("!true")) // { confident: true, value: false }
   894	 *   evaluate(parse("foo + foo")) // { confident: false, value: undefined, deopt: NodePath }
   895	 *

   902	
   903	export function evaluate(
   904	  path: NodePath<>,
   905	  traversalState: StateManager,
   906	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   907	  seen: Map<t.Node, Result> = new Map(),
   908	): $ReadOnly<{

   910	  value: any,
   911	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   912	  reason?: string,
   913	}> {
   914	  const addedImports = importsForState.get(traversalState) ?? new Set();
   915	  importsForState.set(traversalState, addedImports);
   916	
   917	  const state: State = {
   918	    confident: true,
   919	    deoptPath: null,
   920	    seen,
   921	    addedImports,
   922	    functions,
   923	    traversalState,
   924	  };
   925	  let value = evaluateCached(path, state);
   926	  if (!state.confident) value = undefined;
   927

   929	    confident: state.confident,
   930	    deopt: state.deoptPath,
   931	    reason: state.deoptReason,

    36	function isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr: t.Expression): boolean {
    37	  if (t.isTemplateLiteral(expr)) return true;
    38	
    39	  if (
    40	    t.isStringLiteral(expr) ||
    41	    t.isNumericLiteral(expr) ||
    42	    t.isBooleanLiteral(expr)
    43	  )
    44	    return true;
    45	
    46	  if (t.isBinaryExpression(expr)) {
    47	    return ['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', '**'].includes(expr.operator);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  if (t.isUnaryExpression(expr)) {
    51	    return ['-', '+'].includes(expr.operator);
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  if (t.isConditionalExpression(expr)) {
    55	    return (
    56	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.consequent) &&
    57	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.alternate)
    58	    );
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  if (t.isLogicalExpression(expr)) {
    62	    if (expr.operator === '??' || expr.operator === '||') {
    63	      return (
    64	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) || isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    65	      );
    66	    }
    67	    if (expr.operator === '&&') {
    68	      return (
    69	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) && isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    70	      );
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return false;
    75	}
    76	
    77	/// This function looks for `stylex.create` calls and transforms them.
    78	/// 1. It finds the first argument to `stylex.create` and validates it.
    79	/// 2. It pre-processes valid-dynamic parts of style object such as custom presets (spreads)
    80	/// 3. It evaluates the style object to get a JS object. This also handles local constants automatically.
    81	/// 4. It uses the `stylexCreate` from `@stylexjs/shared` to transform the JS
    82	///    object and to get a list of injected styles.
    83	/// 5. It converts the resulting Object back into an AST and replaces the call with it.
    84	/// 6. It also inserts `stylex.inject` calls above the current statement as needed.
    85	export default function transformStyleXCreate(
    86	  path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,

    88	) {

    90

    92	    return;
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  if (
    96	    (node.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    97	      state.stylexCreateImport.has(node.callee.name)) ||
    98	    (node.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    99	      node.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
   100	      node.callee.property.type === 'Identifier' &&

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.

    10	/* eslint-disable no-unused-vars */
    11	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    12	import type { FunctionConfig } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    13	
    14	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    16	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';

    20	  timeUnits,

    25	type TInlineStyles = {
    26	  [string]: {
    27	    +path: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    28	    +originalExpression: t.Expression,
    29	    +expression: t.Expression | t.PatternLike,
    30	  },
    31	};
    32	
    33	type DynamicFns = {
    34	  [string]: [
    35	    +params: Array<t.Identifier>,
    36	    +inlineStyles: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
    37	  ],
    38	};

    40	// This
    41	export function evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
    42	  path: NodePath<>,
    43	  traversalState: StateManager,
    44	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
    45	): $ReadOnly<{
    46	  confident: boolean,
    47	  value: any,
    48	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
    49	  reason?: string,
    50	  fns?: DynamicFns,
    51	}> {
    52	  if (!path.isObjectExpression()) {
    53	    return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  const value: { [string]: mixed } = {};
    57	  const fns: DynamicFns = {};
    58	
    59	  for (const prop of path.get('properties')) {
    60	    if (!prop.isObjectProperty()) {
    61	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    62	    }
    63	    const objPropPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty> = prop;
    64	    const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(objPropPath, traversalState, functions);
    65	    if (!keyResult.confident) {
    66	      return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
    67	    }
    68	    const key = keyResult.value;
    69	
    70	    const valPath = prop.get('value');
    71	    if (!valPath.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
    72	      const val = evaluate(valPath, traversalState, functions);
    73	      if (!val.confident) {
    74	        return val;
    75	      }
    76	      value[key] = val.value;
    77	      continue;
    78	    }
    79	    const fnPath: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression> = valPath;
    80	    const allParams: Array<
    81	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>,
    82	    > = fnPath.get('params');
    83	
    84	    validateDynamicStyleParams(fnPath, allParams);
    85	
    86	    const params: Array<t.Identifier> = allParams
    87	      .filter(
    88	        (
    89	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.SpreadElement>,
    90	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
    91	      )
    92	      .map((param) => param.node);
    93	
    94	    const fnBody = fnPath.get('body');
    95	    if (!fnBody.isObjectExpression()) {
    96	      // We only allow arrow functions without block bodies.
    97	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    98	    }
    99	    const fnObjectBody: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression> = fnBody;
   100	    const evalResult = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   101	      fnObjectBody,
   102	      traversalState,
   103	      functions,
   104	    );
   105	
   106	    if (!evalResult.confident) {
   107	      const { confident, value: v, deopt } = evalResult;
   108	      return { confident, value: v, deopt };
   109	    }
   110	    const { value: v, inlineStyles } = evalResult;
   111	    value[key] = v;
   112	    fns[key] = [params, inlineStyles ?? {}];
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  return { value, confident: true, fns };
   116	}
   117	
   118	function evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   119	  path: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression>,
   120	  traversalState: StateManager,
   121	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   122	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
   123	): $ReadOnly<{
   124	  confident: boolean,
   125	  value: any,
   126	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   127	  reason?: string,
   128	  inlineStyles?: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
   129	}> {
   130	  const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   131	  const inlineStyles: TInlineStyles = {};
   132	  const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   133	    NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   134	  > = path.get('properties');
   135	  for (const prop of props) {
   136	    if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   137	      return { value: null, confident: false };
   138	    }
   139	    if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   140	      const result = evaluate(prop.get('argument'), traversalState, functions);
   141	      if (!result.confident) {
   142	        return result;
   143	      }
   144	      Object.assign(obj, result.value);
   145	      continue;
   146	    }
   147	    if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   148	      const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(prop, traversalState, functions);
   149	      if (!keyResult.confident) {
   150	        return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
   151	      }
   152	      let key = keyResult.value;
   153	      if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
   154	        key = key.slice(4, -1);
   155	      }
   156	
   157	      const valuePath: NodePath<t.Expression | t.PatternLike> =
   158	        prop.get('value');
   159	
   160	      if (valuePath.isObjectExpression()) {
   161	        const result = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   162	          valuePath,
   163	          traversalState,
   164	          functions,
   165	          [...keyPath, key],
   166	        );
   167	        if (!result.confident) {
   168	          return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt, value: null };
   169	        }
   170	        obj[key] = result.value;
   171	        Object.assign(inlineStyles, result.inlineStyles);
   172	      } else {
   173	        const result = evaluate(valuePath, traversalState, functions);
   174	        if (!result.confident) {
   175	          const fullKeyPath = [...keyPath, key];
   176	          const varName =
   177	            '--x-' +
   178	            (keyPath.length > 0
   179	              ? utils.hash([...keyPath, key].join('_'))
   180	              : key);
   181	          obj[key] = `var(${varName})`;
   182	          const node = valuePath.node;
   183	          if (!t.isExpression(node)) {
   184	            throw valuePath.buildCodeFrameError(
   185	              'Expected expression as style value',
   186	              SyntaxError,
   187	            );
   188	          }
   189	          const expression: t.Expression = node as $FlowFixMe;
   190	
   191	          const propName =
   192	            fullKeyPath.find(
   193	              (k) =>
   194	                !k.startsWith(':') && !k.startsWith('@') && k !== 'default',
   195	            ) ?? key;
   196	
   197	          const unit =
   198	            timeUnits.has(propName) || lengthUnits.has(propName)
   199	              ? getNumberSuffix(propName)
   200	              : '';
   201	
   202	          const inlineStyleExpression =
   203	            unit !== ''
   204	              ? t.callExpression(
   205	                  t.arrowFunctionExpression(
   206	                    [t.identifier('val')],
   207	                    t.conditionalExpression(
   208	                      t.binaryExpression(
   209	                        '===',
   210	                        t.unaryExpression('typeof', t.identifier('val')),
   211	                        t.stringLiteral('number'),
   212	                      ),
   213	                      t.binaryExpression(
   214	                        '+',
   215	                        t.identifier('val'),
   216	                        t.stringLiteral(unit),
   217	                      ),
   218	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   219	                        t.binaryExpression(
   220	                          '!=',
   221	                          t.identifier('val'),
   222	                          t.nullLiteral(),
   223	                        ),
   224	                        t.identifier('val'),
   225	                        t.identifier('undefined'),
   226	                      ),
   227	                    ),
   228	                  ),
   229	                  [expression as t.Expression],
   230	                )
   231	              : t.conditionalExpression(
   232	                  t.binaryExpression('!=', expression, t.nullLiteral()),
   233	                  expression,
   234	                  t.identifier('undefined'),
   235	                );
   236	          inlineStyles[varName] = {
   237	            path: [...keyPath, key],
   238	            originalExpression: expression,
   239	            expression: inlineStyleExpression,
   240	          };
   241	        } else {
   242	          obj[key] = result.value;
   243	        }
   244	      }
   245	    }
   246	  }
   247	  return { value: obj, confident: true, inlineStyles };
   248	}
   249	
   250	type KeyResult =
   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}
   278	
   279	function validateDynamicStyleParams(
   280	  path: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression>,
   281	  params: Array<NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>>,
   282	) {
   283	  if (params.some((param) => !param.isIdentifier())) {
   284	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   285	      messages.ONLY_NAMED_PARAMETERS_IN_DYNAMIC_STYLE_FUNCTIONS,
   286	      SyntaxError,
   287	    );
   288	  }
   289	}
   290
